     <h1 class="pg-headline">
      'Scream queen' Marilyn Burns dies, survivor in 'Texas Chainsaw Massacre'
     </h1>
     <div class="metadata ">
      <p class="metadata__byline">
       <span class="metadata__byline__author">
        By Alan Duke, CNN
       </span>
      </p>
      <p class="metadata__show">
      </p>
      <p class="update-time">
       Updated 3:19 PM ET, Wed August 6, 2014
      </p>
      <span class="video__source top_source" id="js-pagetop_video_source">
      </span>
      <div class="m-share m-share__rail-top js-share-rail-top m-share__floating">
       <div id="whatsappIframe" style="display: none;">
       </div>
       <div class="share-bar-whatsapp-container gigya-sharebar-element gig-bar-container gig-share-bar-container" data-social-media-name="whatsapp" data-storyurl="http://www.cnn.com/2014/08/06/showbiz/obit-actress-marilyn-burn/index.html" data-title="'Scream queen' Marilyn Burns dies, survivor in 'Texas Chainsaw Massacre'" data-url="whatsapp://send?text=CNN story:">
        <div class="gig-button-container gig-button-container-count-none gig-button-container-whatsapp gig-share-button-container gig-button-container-horizontal">
         <div class="gig-button gig-share-button gig-button-up gig-button-count-none">
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="js-gigya-sharebar" data-description='Actress Marilyn Burns, a "scream queen" in the original "Texas Chainsaw Massacre," died Tuesday, her manager said. She was 64.' data-image-src="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-t3-entertainment.jpg" data-isshorturl="false" data-link="http://www.cnn.com/2014/08/06/showbiz/obit-actress-marilyn-burn/index.html" data-subtitle="" data-title="'Scream queen' Marilyn Burns dies, survivor in 'Texas Chainsaw Massacre'">
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="pg-rail-tall__wrapper">
      <div class="pg-side-of-rail pg-rail-tall__side">
       <div class="pg-rail-tall__head">
        <section class="zn zn-large-media zn-body zn--idx-0 zn-has-two-containers" data-containers="2" data-eq-pts="xsmall: 0, medium: 460, large: 780, full16x9: 1100" data-vr-zone="zone-0-0" data-zn-id="large-media" id="large-media">
         <div class="l-container">
          <img alt=" Marilyn Burns (center) runs from &quot;Leatherface&quot; in &#39;The Texas Chainsaw Massacre&#39; (1974)." class="media__image media__image--responsive" data-demand-load="not-loaded" data-eq-pts="mini: 0,  xsmall: 221,  small: 308,  medium: 461,  large:  781" data-src-full16x9="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg" data-src-large="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg" data-src-medium="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg" data-src-mini="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-hp-video.jpg" data-src-mini1x1="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-topics.jpg" data-src-small="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-story-top.jpg" data-src-xsmall="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-story-body.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhEAAJAJEAAAAAAP///////wAAACH5BAEAAAIALAAAAAAQAAkAAAIKlI+py+0Po5yUFQA7"/>
          <div class="img__preloader">
          </div>
          <noscript>
           <img alt=" Marilyn Burns (center) runs from &quot;Leatherface&quot; in &#39;The Texas Chainsaw Massacre&#39; (1974)." class="media__image" src="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140526094739-the-texas-chainsaw-massacre-1974-story-top.jpg"/>
          </noscript>
          <div class="media__caption el__gallery_image-title">
           Marilyn Burns (center) runs from "Leatherface" in 'The Texas Chainsaw Massacre' (1974).
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
       </div>
       <div class="pg-rail-tall__body" itemprop="articleBody">
        <section class="zn zn-body-text zn-body zn--idx-0 zn-has-multiple-containers zn-has-13-containers" data-containers="13" data-eq-pts="xsmall: 0, medium: 460, large: 780, full16x9: 1100" data-vr-zone="zone-1-0" data-zn-id="body-text" id="body-text">
         <div class="l-container">
          <div class="el__leafmedia el__leafmedia--storyhighlights el__leafmedia--">
           <div class="el__storyhighlights_wrapper">
            <div class="el__storyhighlights">
             <h3 class="el__headline">
              Story highlights
             </h3>
             <ul class="el__storyhighlights__list">
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               Marilyn Burns was a college student when she landed her "Texas Chainsaw Massacre" role
              </li>
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               Burns portrayed Charles Manson follower Linda Kasabian in TV's "Helter Skelter" mini-series
              </li>
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               Her later career focused on stage productions in Texas
              </li>
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               Moviefone named Burns one of the "10 Sexiest Scream Queens" in 2009
              </li>
             </ul>
            </div>
            <div class="ad ad--epic" data-ad-text="show">
             <div class="ad-ad_ns_btf_01" id="ad_ns_btf_01">
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Actress Marilyn Burns, a "scream queen" in the original "Texas Chainsaw Massacre," died Tuesday, her manager said. She was 64.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           "She was found unresponsive by a family member" in her Houston-area home, manager Chris Roe said.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Burns' acting career began with a small role in Robert Altman's "Brewster McCloud," which was filmed in her hometown of Houston in 1970, according to
           <a href="http://www.horrorscifi.com/2009/01/marilyn-burns-2009-ihsff-hall-of-fame-inductee/" target="_blank">
            her biography published in 2009
           </a>
           when she was inducted into the International Horror &amp; Sci-Fi Film Festival Hall of Fame.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           She was a University of Texas student when she landed the role of Sally Hardesty, the sole survivor in the first "Chainsaw" film in 1974.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           "Chainsaw" director Tobe Hooper also cast Burns in "Eaten Alive" in 1977. She played "a vacationer who unwittingly stumbles upon a hotel run by a madman who feeds his guests to his pet alligator," the biography said.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Her other horror movie roles include "Brutes and Savages"(1977),"Caution: Children at Play"(1981),"Kiss Daddy Goodbye" (1981) and "Future-Kill" (1985).
          </p>
          <div class="el__gallery--standard js__gallery--standard js__leafmedia--gallery">
           <div class="js__gallery__close--standard el__gallery__close--standard el__storyelements--close">
           </div>
           <div class="el__gallery--teaseimage">
            <div class="el__resize">
             <div class="el__position media js-gallery-aspect-ratio-wrapper">
              <img alt="Click through to see&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.cnn.com/SPECIALS/world/obituaries-2014&quot;&gt; people who died&lt;/a&gt; in 2014." class="media__image media__image--responsive media__image--cut-format" data-cut-format="Horizontal Gallery" data-demand-load="not-loaded" data-eq-pts="mini: 0,  xsmall: 221,  small: 308,  medium: 461,  large:  781" data-src-full16x9="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-horizontal-large-gallery.jpeg" data-src-large="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-horizontal-large-gallery.jpeg" data-src-medium="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-horizontal-large-gallery.jpeg" data-src-mini="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-horizontal-large-gallery.jpeg" data-src-mini1x1="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-topics.jpeg" data-src-small="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-horizontal-large-gallery.jpeg" data-src-xsmall="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/141204183726-people-we-lost-2014-final-horizontal-large-gallery.jpeg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhEAAJAJEAAAAAAP///////wAAACH5BAEAAAIALAAAAAAQAAkAAAIKlI+py+0Po5yUFQA7"/>
              <div class="img__preloader">
              </div>
              <noscript>

                , the man whose voice introduced the cast of NBC's "Saturday Night Live" for decades, died at the age of 96, the network announced August 19.
               </span>

                , the Swiss surrealist artist whose works of sexual-industrial imagery and design of the eponymous creature in the "Alien" movies were known around the world, died on May 12. He was 74.
               </span>
              </div>

                , the middleweight boxing contender who was wrongly convicted of a triple murder in New Jersey in the 1960s, died April 20 at the age of 76, according to Win Wahrer, the director of client services for the Association in Defence of the Wrongly Convicted.
               </span>
              </div>

                <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/02/15/showbiz/john-henson-dies/index.html">
                 John Henson
                </a>
                , the son of Jim Henson who is perhaps most notable for his portrayal of Sweetums on "The Muppets," died after a "sudden, massive heart attack," his family's company said on February 15.
               </span>

              <div class="media__caption el__gallery_image-title">
               <span class="media__caption-head">
                People we lost in 2014
               </span>
               
               <span class="el__storyelement__gray">
                Legendary folk singer
                <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/01/28/showbiz/pete-seeger-death/index.html" target="_blank">
                 Pete Seeger
                </a>
                , known for classics such as  "Where Have All the Flowers Gone" and "If I Had a Hammer (The Hammer Song)," died of natural causes in New York on January 27, his grandson told CNN. He was 94.

             /* jshint browser: true, node: false *//* globals jQuery, CNN */'use strict';jQuery(document).ready(function () {var galleryAdSlide = new CNN.AdSlide('el__gallery', false, CNN.contentModel.singletonFile);});
            </script>
           </div>
           <div class="el__gallery__expand--standard el__storyelements--expand">
            EXPAND GALLERY
           </div>
          </div>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Burns played a real-life character in the 1976 television miniseries "Helter Skelter."  She portrayed Charles Manson follower Linda Kasabian, who testified against the cult leader and other members at their murder trial.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           She was given a cameo role in the 1994 "Texas Chainsaw Massacre" remake, but her later career focused on stage productions in Texas.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Moviefone named Burns one of the
           <a href="http://news.moviefone.com/2009/09/09/sexiest-horror-scream-queens/" target="_blank">
            "10 Sexiest Scream Queens" in a list published in 2009
           </a>
           , citing her "vulnerability (and hotness, natch) feels as real as can be."
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2008/SHOWBIZ/Movies/06/27/top10horror.tsr/index.html">
            Top 10 horrific movie moments
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           <a href="http://www.cnn.com/SPECIALS/world/obituaries-2014/index.html" target="_blank">
            People we've lost in 2014
           </a>
          </p>
         </div>
        </section>
        <div class="pg-body__social">
        </div>

                 <img alt="FILE - This is a  Nov. 27, 2005 file photo of author P.D. James  as she discusses her latest novel, &quot;The Lighthouse,&quot; another mystery featuring Scotland Yard detective Adam Dalgliesh, during an interview in New York. Publisher Faber and Faber says mystery writer P.D. James, who brought realistic modern characters to the classical British detective story died Thursday Nov. 27, 2014 . She was 94. James&#39; books, many featuring sleuth Adam Dalgliesh, sold millions in many countries and most were just as popular when adapted for television.
